 The Supreme Court on Tuesday slammed the central government for not being 'serious' in formulating a policy to curb its sale with the intention of stopping the incidents of acid attacks
 nyaayamurti aaram lodha kii adhyakshata vaali khandpeeth ne sarkaar ke ravaiye par naaraazgi vyakt karte hue kaha ki tejaab ke hamalon se rojaanaa log mar rahe hai, lekin nyaayalay ko 16 ko ashwasan dene ke baavjood kendra is bare main niti taiyaar karne main vifal rahaa he
 The judges, while consulting the state governments, gave the central government a week's time to formulate the policy, saying, "there is no seriousness of the government towards this issue
" ’’ nyaayadhishon ne kaha, ‘‘log mar rahe hai lekin aapako isaki parvaah nahin he
 Think of the people who are losing their lives every day

 nyaayalay ne isse pehle 6 farvari ko kendra sarkaar ko chah saptaah ke bheetar sabhi rajyon or kendra shasit pradeshon ke mukhya sachivon kii baithak bulaane or uske tejaab kii bikri niyantrit karne ke tareekon, tejaab ke hamalon ke shikaar logon ke upachaar, unke liye muaavja or punarvaas ke muddon par vichaar karne kaa nirdesh diya tha
